‚óŹ Good scan. Let me add my own findings on top.

  ---
  CRITICAL / HIGH

  1. FridgeScreen never explicitly tasked ‚ÄĒ Phase 2 builds InventoryList
  component but no task says "build FridgeScreen". BottomNav points to it, tests
  assume it exists. Missing task.
  2. DatePicker mock blocks onChange ‚ÄĒ jest.setup.js mock returns plain View and
  doesn't forward onChange. ReviewScreen.test.js line 1422 fires onChange to
  set past date ‚ÄĒ test will always pass vacuously (date never changes,
  validation never triggers). Broken test.
  3. Phase 5 ScanScreen.lock.test.js not updated ‚ÄĒ PLAN says update
  ScanScreen.test.js mock target from mockScanReceipt ‚Üí scanReceipt.
  ScanScreen.lock.test.js also mocks @/utils/mockScanReceipt ‚ÄĒ omitted from the
  update instruction. Will break in Phase¬†5.
  4. expo-document-picker not globally mocked ‚ÄĒ TESTS.md global setup doesn't
  mock it. ProfileScreen imports it; its test file will throw on module load.
  All ProfileScreen.test.js tests fail.
  5. RateLimitError class not exported from scanReceipt ‚ÄĒ test defines it
  locally and checks err.name. ScanScreen must check err.name === 
  'RateLimitError' (not instanceof). Plan never states this. Easy to implement
  wrong.

  ---
  MEDIUM

  6. Notification integration in InventoryContext untested ‚ÄĒ Phase 5 wires
  scheduleExpiryNotification / cancelExpiryNotification into every CRUD op. No
  test covers this. Could be silently skipped.
  7. InventoryItem quick actions untested ‚ÄĒ Plan says Fridge has "mark Consumed
  / Wasted" quick actions per item. InventoryItem tests only check display. Zero
  action coverage.
  8. Review ‚Üí Fridge navigation type ‚ÄĒ ReviewScreen calls navigate('Fridge').
  Fridge is a tab, Review is a stack screen above tabs. Must use
  navigation.navigate('BottomTabs', { screen: 'Fridge' }) or equivalent ‚ÄĒ plain
  navigate('Fridge') may push a new stack screen instead of switching tabs.
  9. Day-3 boundary ambiguous ‚ÄĒ Plan: "Expiring Soon = 0‚Äď3 days inclusive".
  InventoryItem test uses day 2 ‚Üí warning, day 60 ‚Üí safe. No test at exactly 3
  days. Off-by-one risk in implementation.
  10. Onboarding import needs expo-document-picker ‚ÄĒ Plan says "Import Backup"
  option on Onboarding (Phase¬†2) but expo-document-picker not installed/wired
  until Phase¬†5. Either move picker to Phase 2 or remove the Onboarding import
  option until Phase¬†5.
  11. updateItem should update updatedAt ‚ÄĒ Auto-delete logic purges by
  updatedAt. If user edits an item (expiry date fix), updatedAt must refresh.
  Plan spec doesn't require this. Edge case: recently edited items get
  incorrectly purged.
  12. Notification trigger date is timezone-sensitive ‚ÄĒ
  scheduleExpiryNotification test compares trigger.date to new 
  Date('2026-06-09') (UTC midnight). On non-UTC machines this will be 11pm
  previous day. Test is brittle.
  13. setupFilesAfterFramework jest config key ‚ÄĒ TESTS.md line 21 uses
  setupFilesAfterFramework. Correct Jest key is setupFilesAfterFramework. Typo
  breaks test setup entirely ‚ÄĒ mocks never register.

  ---
  LOW / UX

  14. stat-expired testID expects raw number children ‚ÄĒ StatCard animates count
  via Reanimated withTiming. Test reads props.children as Number. Reanimated
  mock makes this synchronous so it works, but if you ever swap to JS Animated,
  it breaks silently.
  15. History screen back navigation ‚ÄĒ History is accessible from Profile only.
  Tests mock goBack but PLAN's navigation setup puts History in the stack above
  tabs. TopAppBar onBack must be wired ‚ÄĒ not mentioned in History screen build
  task.

  ---
  Top 3 to fix immediately before Phase 2: #1 (add FridgeScreen task), #2 (fix 
  DatePicker mock), #13 (fix jest key typo). Rest can be addressed per-phase.
  ‚éŅ ¬†Stop says: Review gates: Phase 2 -> cavecrew-reviewer | Phase 4 -> verify skill | Phase 5 -> security-review skill

‚ĚĮ how can i check dev mode app?                                                 

‚óŹ Two options:

  Option 1 ‚ÄĒ Expo Go (fastest, no build needed)
  1. Install Expo Go on your phone (iOS App Store / Google Play)
  2. Phone and PC must be on same WiFi
  3. Scan QR code with:
    - iOS: Camera app
    - Android: Expo Go app ‚Üí Scan QR

  Option 2 ‚ÄĒ Android emulator (no phone needed)
  # Install Android Studio, then:
  npx expo start --android

  Option 3 ‚ÄĒ iOS simulator (Mac only)
  npx expo start --ios

  Expo Go is fastest. Just install it, scan, done.
  ‚éŅ ¬†Stop says: Review gates: Phase 2 -> cavecrew-reviewer | Phase 4 -> verify skill | Phase 5 -> security-review skill

‚úĽ Cooked for 9s

‚ĚĮ on my phone it says project is incompatible with this version of expo go but  
  i downloaded the latest in the app store                                      

‚óŹ SDK 56 is too new ‚ÄĒ Expo Go on App Store likely supports SDK 52 or 53 max. Two
  fixes:

  Option 1 ‚ÄĒ Downgrade to SDK 51 (PLAN spec, guaranteed Expo Go support)
  npx create-expo-app@sdk-51 --template blank
  But that means re-scaffolding. Better to just downgrade expo in package.json.

  Option 2 ‚ÄĒ Use development build (recommended, works with any SDK)
  npm install -g eas-cli
  eas login
  eas build:configure
  eas build -p android --profile preview
  Install the resulting APK on your phone. No Expo Go needed.

  Option 3 ‚ÄĒ Check what SDK your Expo Go supports
  Open Expo Go ‚Üí tap the Expo logo ‚Üí shows supported SDK versions. Then tell me
  and I'll downgrade to match.

  Option 4 ‚ÄĒ Web preview (instant, no phone needed)
  npx expo start --web
  Opens in browser. Not full native but good for UI testing.

  Which do you want?
  ‚éŅ ¬†Stop says: Review gates: Phase 2 -> cavecrew-reviewer | Phase 4 -> verify skill | Phase 5 -> security-review skill
